The reason why the black belt has "UInvDefaultItemType = belt" is because its name ("black belt") is not the same as its item type ("belt"). The "UInvDefaultItemType" property preserves that item type in order to save memory and reduce the size of the save data. This means that this is a variable item, which also meanings that it needs to have a "UInvVariableType" property. Because of the "UInvVariableType" property that this item has, UInv will try to group items of this same type together if they are completely identical (other than their quantity), otherwise it will create a new stack of items. Keep clicking the "add" button below to see how the matching items automatically stack together. Since variable items may have multiple item names, you can find the variable items by looking for items of that default type.
